--- Commit Message ---
LU-12846 mdd: return error while delete failed

Since we use a global buffer, So avoid to replace the
index name while iterate the orphan directory. Also
return error code in mdd_orphan_destroy while dt_delete
failed. Else will cause a dead loop.

Fixes: e1ace3751f ("LU-8514 mdd: transaction failure should be checked")
Signed-off-by: Yang Sheng <ys@whamcloud.com>

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2019-11-01 11:02:20.000000000) ---
Patch Set 1:

(1 comment)

I think the goal is if there is an -ENOENT error deleting a file, then the file is already deleted, and there is little value to cause a failure in this case since the file is already gone we wanted.  It is better to continue on as if there was no error at all.

Patch Set 6: Code-Review-1

(4 comments)

I think this still isn't really solving the problem, because it is still printing a mostly-useless error message for "rc = -ENOENT" and it is still being returned to the caller.

This should quietly drop -ENOENT if it is hit, because there is no value to complain that a file doesn't exist while trying to delete it.
